【SVI Bataan - In case of evaluated receipt settlement, please enter tax code】
问题: SVI Bataan - In case of evaluated receipt settlement, please enter tax code

根因分类: SAP Program / Configuration Error

具体根因: Software - SAP Issue

问题描述: Reference Order:
RO25BA0103 
RO25BA0154
 
0328]SVI SAN FERNANDO

Error:POHEADER : Purchase order still contains faulty items 
POITEM : In case of evaluated receipt settlement, please enter tax code

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Issue: Integration - Vendor tagged as FFD.
Resolution:
1. The store must submit a request letter to OPC for settlement.
2. OPC should simply post movement 311 in SAP (from storage location 0003 to 0001) to reverse the inventory.
3. In DMall system, OPC can then process a 171 (add) in storage location 0001 and a 170 (deduct) in storage location 0003.
4. DMall will update the reference order RO25BA0103 & RO25BA0154 status to "No Need" in the "Order Query."
Masterdata may tag vendor 120916 in SAP as "FFD" so that the article will be tagged as "non-returnable" in DMall.

【POS HUNG UP when processing OFFLINE CREDIT and QRPH】

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:​
Encountered pos hung up when processing offline credit and qrph at SSM Jmall. As advise for this we re start the pos then process again after re starting

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue: POS keeps on loading when a cashier cancels or press the "x" button and then selects another payment method.

Root Cause Analysis:Defect from DMall
The issue occurs when selecting a payment method with a pop-up window on the right side (e.g., QRPH, offline BDO Credit etc).
If the cashier cancels or press the "x" button and then selects another payment method, the system enters an indefinite loading state (refer to the screenshot below)

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2. R&D confirmed that the issue occurs in thenew POS version 1.0.4.5 (202511_1_November Special).3.The upgrade to POS version 1.0.4.5 has been temporarily suspended to prevent further impact on other POS terminals.4.As discussed with the SM IT team, the version of the POS that have already been upgraded will not be rolled back to the previous version.
5.R&D fixed the issue in the newPOS version 1.0.4.6 and then released it to the Prod Environment.
6. All stores and POS units have been updated, and the issue has not been encountered again.Resolved the ticket.

【The D mall app with 1.0.4.3 Version need to update to 1.0.4.4 Version, t will be apply to all POS in SM- Fairview Hyper market.】
问题: The D mall app with 1.0.4.3 Version need to update to 1.0.4.4 Version, t will be apply to all POS in SM- Fairview Hyper market.

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Inquiry / Knowledge

问题描述: Type:The D mall app with 1.0.4.3 Version need to update to 1.0.4.4 VersionResponse Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:November 19, 2025

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:​User KnowledgeThe upgrade to POS version 1.0.4.5 has been temporarily suspended to prevent further impact on other POS terminals.


Issue Description:The D mall app with 1.0.4.3 Version need to update to 1.0.4.4 Version, t will be apply to all POS in SM- Fairview Hyper market.


Troubleshooting process:
We would like to inform you about an issue reported by the store last night, 11/18/2025, regarding the new POS version 1.0.4.5 (202511_1_November Special).

Investigation:
1.As confirmed by our R&D team and validated in UAT, the issue occurs when selecting a payment method with a pop-up window on the right side (e.g., QRPH, offline BDO Credit etc).
If the cashier cancels or press the "x" button and then selects another payment method, the system enters an indefinite loading state.
2. This issue does not occur in the previous POS version 1.0.4.3.



Action Taken:
1. The upgrade to POS version 1.0.4.5 has been temporarily suspended to prevent further impact on other POS terminals.
2. A total of 688 POS have already been successfully upgraded.

Next Steps:
1.As per our discussions with the SM IT team, the version of the POS that have already been upgraded will not be rolled back to the previous version.
2.Our R&D team is working on a fix and aims to release it to UAT tonight, upon SM approval.

【NUTRI ASIA UNGR ITEMS】
问题: NUTRI ASIA UNGR ITEMS

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request Un Grd items of NUTRI ASIA ,INC.
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:11/19/2025​

P.O # 1106811603GR # 5111829308

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Upon checking in both SAP and Dmall, PO 1106811603 has multiple GR entries, specifically 5111829308 and 5111826366, while the store provided only 5111829308 as the GR number for this PO. All articles in the PO were received in both SAP and Dmall, yet the store reported that only 15 out of 20 articles were GR’d. Confirmed by Sir Edelito that all articles plan quantity under PO 1106811603 was delivered with two receipt. This issue occurred due to user error, as the store referenced only one GR number and overlooked the additional GR entry, which led to the incorrect assumption of missing items. I informed Sir Edelito that the PO had multiple receipts and that all articles were already completely received.

Affected Markets User:

解决方案:
Define Issue:SMCo M ALVAREZ LAS PIÑAS [1576] Integration Inventory 2025 November 21 - Error Msg: Fail to transfer stock place.
Root Cause Analysis:Defect from DMall

Resolution:
We found an integration error in dashboard and created a ticket and coordinated the issue to our R&D.
Based on our investigation, the RPO was submitted in the PDA even though the inventory of the article is 0.
This was confirmed a bug in the system and added it to our problem management as problem #244.
For short-term solution, we tagged the order number to "No need".
This will be added toProblem List No. 244.
A fix will be implemented to ensure that when submitting returned goods via the PDA, the return quantity cannot be less than or equal to zero.

Create an Integration ticket.
Coordinated to Functional.a. The store will submit a request letter to OPC.

b. OPC will process the request using two approaches:

i. In DMall: Process movement type 170 (deduct) in storage location 0003 and movement type 171 (add) in storage location 0001.

For RO259T0522
Articles: 20192799 and 20243592
Qty: 10 pieces each.

For RO25970313
Articles: 20540112
Qty: 10 pieces

ii. In SAP: Process movement type 311 from storage location 0003 to 0001.

We cannot process a direct movement type 311 in DMall because the vendor is already flagged as "for deletion" in SAP, and it could trigger another integration error.

c. DMall will tag the reference order (RO259T0522 andRO25970313) to remove the error from the dashboard.
Proceed on resolving

【cannot open dmall app】
问题: cannot open dmall app

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Restart

问题描述: Type: cannot open DMall app
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue: cannot open DMall App​

解决摘要: Log to Problem

解决方案:
Define Issue:cannot open dmall app​

Root Cause Analysis: Defect from DMall

Resolution:
- Acknowledged the ticket.
-Coordinate with our R&D.
-According to our R&D Team, based on the POS logs, the cashier initiated a refund transaction on POS#038 at 2025-11-23 22:36:58. This event serves as the starting point for the subsequent issue observed on the POS.
-After completing the refund transaction on POS#038, POS#038 experienced an abnormal restart within milliseconds at 2025-11-23 22:36:59. This sudden restart disrupted normal operations and impacted the POS local database sequence.
-Upon checking the Continuous Ping logs for POS#038, we confirmed that there are no available records for November 23, 2025. Furthermore, we confirmed that this POS did not undergo or encounter any Windows Update during the said period.
-Note:Due to the abnormal restart of POS#038, the POS local database was unable to update or increment properly. This resulted in the SI number not increasing as expected, which then triggered the SI# Continuity exception message on the POS.
-Solution:
Temporary Solution:Our R&D Team will proceed with adjusting the sequence in the POS local database. The current sequence value is 00044, which needs to be updated to 00045 to align with the correct SI progression.This adjustment will ensure that when the POS is used again, the system will generate the next SI number as 00044, maintaining proper sequence continuity.
Long-Term Solution: The SI exception is actually a safeguard designed for the POS to prevent SI discontinuity. If discontinuity is detected, the POS cannot be used — this is by design. We will continue to optimize the SI exception handling.
Our R&D Team will continue to enhance and refine the mechanism for handling SI# continuity exceptions to reduce the likelihood of similar issues occurring in the future. These improvements aim to strengthen system reliability and ensure proper SI continuity across all transactions.
-Our R&D has successfully resolved the issue related to the SI# continuity exception for SVI Makati POS#038.
-We already advise the store to use the POS.
-The ticket is resolved.

Data Collection/References:-

【REQUEST FOR REGENERATION OF ARC POS FILE】
问题: REQUEST FOR REGENERATION OF ARC POS FILE

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Software - Application Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:​


Good Day, 

We would like to request for the regeneration of the ARC POS file of 5035 SVI STTB for Nov. 20, 2025 Transaction Date because there's no file created a

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:There is a bug where if multiple regenerate EOD tasks are triggered within a 40-minute window, some of the tasks may become blocked or fail to enter the processing queue.​​


Issue Description:REQUEST FOR REGENERATION OF ARC POS FILE​


Troubleshooting process:
1.Acknowledge the ticket.
2.Report in our R&D Team.
3.There is a bug where if multiple regenerate EOD tasks are triggered within a 40-minute window, some of the tasks may become blocked or fail to enter the processing queue.
4. When this situation occurs, the program will randomly select a regenerate EOD tasks. If the selected task is the one with the problem, it will not run properly and will block other regenerate EOD tasks.
5. Only by waiting for the next full 10 minutes can the program continue to randomly select the next task.  
6. We added this in Problem Management No#276 for further investigation and to improve the monitoring in order to prevent this problem from occurring again.
7. Our R&D Team re-push the task and SM IT confirmed that the ARC File already exist. 
​8. Resolved.

【SITE DESCRIPTION NOT SYNCHRONIZE IN DMALL SCREEN】
问题: SITE DESCRIPTION NOT SYNCHRONIZE IN DMALL SCREEN

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Inquiry / Knowledge

问题描述: Dear DMALL Support,

May we request to check and validate the site description of[6581]SMCo SANTIAGO 3 displayed inRetail Price Queryand other related screen with site description.
Please see screenshot

Thank You,
Edith
IT F

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:User Knowledge - inform the requester regarding the logic of the system.


Issue Description:SITE DESCRIPTION NOT SYNCHRONIZE IN DMALL SCREEN​

Troubleshooting process:
According to our R&D Team, the site name in the search box allows users to fill in the site code, site status, and site name. The (Invalidate)purpose is to indicate when a site is unavailable, helping to prevent users from generating incorrect business. However, on the page (especially in the list item/column), it only shows the site code and site name.



For your other concern regarding on the Store Article Mgt, the reason for not having the invalidate word isbecause Store Article Mgt have not use the site component.

【REQUEST FOR REGENERATION OF ARC POS FILE】
问题: REQUEST FOR REGENERATION OF ARC POS FILE

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

Good Day, 

We would like to request for the regeneration of the ARC POS file of 0327 SVI CON for Nov. 21, 2025 Transaction Date because there's no file created at .

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:There is a bug where if multiple regenerate EOD tasks are triggered within a 40-minute window, some of the tasks may become blocked or fail to enter the processing queue.​​


Issue Description:REQUEST FOR REGENERATION OF ARC POS FILE​


Troubleshooting process:
1.Acknowledge the ticket.
2.Report in our R&D Team.
3.There is a bug where if multiple regenerate EOD tasks are triggered within a 40-minute window, some of the tasks may become blocked or fail to enter the processing queue.
4. When this situation occurs, the program will randomly select a regenerate EOD tasks. If the selected task is the one with the problem, it will not run properly and will block other regenerate EOD tasks.
5. Only by waiting for the next full 10 minutes can the program continue to randomly select the next task.  
6. We added this in Problem Management No#276 for further investigation and to improve the monitoring in order to prevent this problem from occurring again.
7. Our R&D Team re-push the task and SM IT confirmed that the ARC File already exist. 
​8. Resolved.

4.In line with this, the issue has been logged underProblem No. 271, and we will proceed with resolving all related Manage Engine tickets.

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:Request to Adjust Invty & Tag Ref Order as "No Need"Module
tenant id
Branch
receiving order
sap no.
date
Annual Pcount
  Date
Status
Findings

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
SVI Tuguegarao 
The error occurred because valuation data for material 10223807 was locked by user MD4ANGEL. Following the standard resolution for recurring locks, R&D reprocessed the order, which automatically updated the SAP status to “YES.” The reference order was adjusted in Dmall using movement type 170 and tagged as “No Need.” This process has been confirmed with OPC and the Functional team.

SVI - BF Paranaque
On December 7, 2024, a TP-311 transaction of 48 pieces (SLOC 0001 → SLOC 0002) was successfully posted in SAP. On December 21, 2024, a TP-311 transaction of 60 pieces (SLOC 0002 → SLOC 0001) exceeded the available inventory in SLOC 0002, creating a 12-piece deficit. This transaction was not posted in SAP but was reflected in Dmall. On January 3, 2025, a TP-311 of 12 pieces (SLOC 0001 → SLOC 0002) posted successfully in both SAP and Dmall, offsetting the deficit.

1. The store should submit a request letter to OPC for settlement.
2. OPC will perform TP-311 (from SLOC 2 to SLOC 1) with 60 pieces in SAP.
3. Dmall has already tagged the reference order as “NO NEED.”

Article Type:Consignment without

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

【ROVING POS ERROR】
问题: ROVING POS ERROR

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Program Bug

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

Happy To Serve,

Please assist us regarding our roving pos use in mall set up, we encountered problem while transacted the 1st customer with note in pos "Pos ha

解决摘要: Log to Problem

解决方案:
Define Issue:SSM Sucat Roving POS 701 was expected to remain active for15 daysinSSM Sucat [0062](fromNovember 16, 2025 to November 30, 2025).
However, the device automatically returned toSSM Head Office [0100]after only14 daysonNovember 29, 2025.

Root Cause Analysis:The issue was caused by a time zone calculation bug. The system incorrectly converts the roving POS activation time fromUTC to Manila time.
Around the daily cutoff time (23:59:50 Manila time), the system subtracts an extra 8 hours resulting in incorrect date calculations.
As a result, roving POS units that areactivated before 08:00:00 Manila timeare mistakenly counted as if they were activated one day earlier.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket.
2. DMall R&D team confirmed that the issue was caused by a time zone calculation bug.
3. Added the issue toProblem 282.
4. Informed the store and SM team about the impact and temporary workaround to avoid this issue.
5. Advised themactivate the roving POSafter 08:00:00 Manila time, preferably between08:00:00 and 16:00:00.​Resolved the ticket.
Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:

Seal# :3396777-82

解决方案:
Root Cause:
Based on checking, we confirmed there is a changed in the DNs of SEAL#3396777-82. The DNs under the affected seal was first GI on 11/25/2025 and was downloaded to DMall system the next day. Then on 11/29/2025 these DNs were reversed and was GI again on the same day.

【DMALL - Unable to print grs】
问题: DMALL - Unable to print grs

根因分类: Support Group Error

具体根因: Others

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

Unable to print grs of century pacific food, inc. with p.o #1106687810 due to partial gr issue.

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
ROOT CAUSE:PO No. 1106687810 was created and released on Oct. 22, 2025, with a scheduled delivery date of Dec. 02, 2025. As reflected in SAP, user NHOSCHSU18 deleted article numbers 20580672 due to an INTERCHANGE BARCODE issue, as indicated by the Supply Chain. This update was formally communicated to the stores through an email advisory. For further information, please refer to the advisory issued by Supply Chain. In accordance with SOP, the store must return the affected items to the vendor. 

To resolve this issue:

1. The store should submit a request letter for settlement to OPC.
2. OPC will perform the "undo" process, which will automatically reverse the transaction and update the reference order status to "no need."


A long-term solution has already been implemented, allowing the "undo" function to be performed at the article level.

【cannot print item barcode in shelf label】

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type: Incident
Response Level:Level D
Details of Issue:

Happy to serve !
Please be informed that we cannot print item barcode in shelftag. The dmall is asking for a seasonal code in which we do not know where to get it. Attached is

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:cannot print item barcode in shelf labelRoot Cause Analysis:Defect From DMall/ User Procedural problem

Resolution:
Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated the issue to our R&D.
In our initial investigation, the reason the error message"No applicable template, Please reach out to implementation team for help" showed up is because article20121540 doesn't have the label "Season Code".
After informing the store of our findings, they mentioned that they usually use the template “Item barcode with price printed by 3’s.”Upon conducting further investigation, we found that the templates “Item barcode with price printed by 3’s” and “Item barcode without price printed by 3’s” were disabled by an SM employee, which resulted in the store being unable to use these templates.
We coordinated this to SM side and asked an approval to revert back the changes.
After we got the approval, DMall manually reverted the changes and the store can now use the templates.
Proceeds in resolving the ticket.

09686165958

dmall2helpdesk@dmall.com

FRG0023

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:SVI Tarlac [0868] IBMS Integration logs 2025 December 4 - Error Msg: Movement type 933: Deficit of SL Unrestricted-use 2 PC : 20537626 0868 0003

Root Cause:User error

Resolution:
We found an integration error in Dashboard and made a ticket.
Based on our investigation, articles 20537626 doesn't have enough storage for the inventory movement in DMall that's why the error shows.
Coordinated with Functional team, and based on them, upon checking in SAP,there are some transactions that were perform by user NHOOPCVP01 on 10/22/2025. These transactions has no touch point in DMall since it was perform in SAP resulting to inventory discrepancy.
Based on OPC Ma'am Zha,This was originally a settlement request from the store for an archived article with floating system inventory in SAP only, which is why the settlement was processed through SAP. However, an RO posting the following day created an inventory adjustment from SLOC‑1 to SLOC‑3 in DMALL. This resulted in a negative balance of 2 pcs in SLOC‑1. In any case, the concern was already settled on December 1, 2025.
Based on Functional team,the affected article has already been archived. To resolve this issue, and considering that the inventory for the affected article has been fully zeroed out and the article has been delisted from site SVI Tarlac, we kindly request that the SAP post status of the affected article be updated to “No Need.”
DMall already tagged the affected article as No need.
We will now proceed in resolving this ticket.

sto# 2035335919 DN#74399250 ( 0800_SMCO BALIWAG)

It should be to new store ( 6996

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause Analysis:it was confirmed that the store processed wrong site code (SMCo Baliwag) for created STO.

Resolution:

2. OPC will reverse the Goods Issue in SAP.
3. OPC will delete the DN (74399250) in SAP.
4. OPC will do 171 mvt in SLoc1 for the affected articles.
5. DMall will tag the Sap Post Status to 'no need'.​

【[0873] SVI San Pablo : GR - STO from DC (still posting status)】
问题: [0873] SVI San Pablo : GR - STO from DC (still posting status)

根因分类: SAP Program / Configuration Error

具体根因: Software - SAP Issue

问题描述: Issue: The transaction status remains as “Posting” even though the transaction was initiated on December 3 at 5:57 PM.
Details:
Reference Order: ID10873202512030002
Seal Numbers: 0683791-92
Shipper: [2173] SVI Banlic Depot
Recipient: [0873] SVI San

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Issue: Order Number (STO) has status of pending for posting.
Resolution: After further checking, we found that the posting issue is due to the deleted DN 0074691502 by DC Banlic, associated with seal 0683791-92. The store confirmed that the DN contains actual items.
To resolve this issue promptly, please follow these steps:
The store should submit a formal request letter to OPC with the affected STO number, DN, and articles with quantities.
Once the Goods Receipt is available in SAP, DMall will update the GR in the DMall system for the affected DN and articles.
